Welcome to the lost diaries of different worlds, DiamondMage!
Our goal is to try to put the pieces together
located within this document of lost text: are the diary entries, dates and at times: an inventory list
Enjoy your reading, enjoy your time. May the thing you are looking , be found in these lines
